### [1] [Dynamical Completion of Coupling-Charge Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30707)
*Kamal Hajian,Bayram Tekin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了标量-规范场耦合格局的一种局域动力学完备化方案：通过构建由拓扑形式场强与引力拉格朗日密度之差构成的“缺陷”动能项，使辅助标量场成为传播的有质量自由度，同时确保热力学耦合常数仍作为守恒积分常数而非局域变化场存在。在常数耦合构型下，辅助应力-能量贡献完全消失，完美保持原始黑洞解、第一定律和Smarr关系。以宇宙学常数和高斯-博内耦合为例进行了说明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原标量-规范场耦合格局中，辅助标量场被限制为刚性、非动力学的构型，缺乏局域动力学自由度。作者旨在引入一种局域、动力学的完备化方案，使标量场能够作为有质量自由度传播，同时保持热力学耦合常数的守恒积分特性。

Method: 从缺陷（拓扑形式场强与引力拉格朗日密度之差）构造动能项，使标量场成为传播的有质量自由度；该局域扇区作为电荷守恒的有质量标量反作用，确保热力学耦合保持为守恒积分常数而非局域变化场。

Result: 在常数耦合构型下，辅助应力-能量贡献完全消失，原始黑洞解、第一定律和Smarr关系得以完美保持。以宇宙学常数和高斯-博内耦合为例验证了该构造的有效性。

Conclusion: 该局域动力学完备化方案成功将标量-规范场耦合格局推广到动力学情形，既赋予了标量场传播自由度，又保留了热力学耦合作为守恒积分常数的核心特征，为扩展黑洞热力学提供了更完整的理论基础。

Abstract: The scalar-gauge pair formulation promotes gravitational coupling constants to conserved charges, clarifying their role in extended black hole thermodynamics. However, its original incarnation restricts these auxiliary scalar fields to rigid, non-dynamical configurations. In this paper, we introduce a local, dynamical completion of this framework. By constructing the kinetic sector from a defect, which is the difference between the top-form field strength and the associated gravitational Lagrangian density, we allow the scalar to propagate as a genuine massive degree of freedom. Crucially, this local sector acts as a charge-preserving massive scalar backreaction, ensuring the thermodynamic coupling remains a conserved integration constant rather than a locally varying field. When evaluated on constant-coupling configurations, the auxiliary stress-energy contributions vanish entirely, perfectly preserving the original black hole solutions, the first law, and the Smarr relation. We illustrate this construction using the cosmological constant and the Gauss-Bonnet coupling.

</details>


### [2] [Ray tracing ultracompact boson stars: visibility modulations and incomplete photon rings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30729)
*Seppe J. Staelens,Ece Alkan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究非克尔光子环在事件视界望远镜成像中的可探测性，通过对球对称和旋转的超致密孤立子玻色星进行光线追踪成像，发现清晰的可见度振幅调制仅存在于球对称情况且限于特定观测倾角范围，表明这种调制不能作为超致密黑洞模拟器的普遍特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在克尔黑洞光子环结构已被充分理解的背景下，探究未来EHT成像能否约束非克尔光子环的存在，以及额外光子环通过可见度振幅低频调制呈现的可能性。

Method: 对球对称和旋转的稳定及不稳定超致密孤立子玻色星进行光线追踪成像，在傅里叶空间（可见度振幅）中分析低频调制特征。

Result: 清晰调制仅出现在球对称情形且限于特定观测倾角范围；旋转玻色星的光子环不完整，且可能需要不稳定的顺行光环来弥补。

Conclusion: 可见度振幅的低频调制不能作为超致密黑洞模拟器的普遍预期特征。

Abstract: Modified black holes and black hole mimickers can give rise to additional photon rings in ray-traced images. With the photon ring structure of Kerr well understood, the question arises how well future versions of the Event Horizon Telescope images would be able to constrain the presence of non-Kerr photon rings. In this work, we investigate how likely additional photon rings are to present themselves through low-frequency modulations of the visibility amplitude, i.e. in Fourier space where the data live. To this end, we generate ray-traced images of stable and unstable ultracompact, solitonic boson stars, both in spherical symmetry and with rotation. We find that clear modulations in the associated visibility amplitude are only present in spherical symmetry, for a restricted range of observer inclinations, hence suggesting that these modulations can not be a generic expectation of ultracompact black-hole mimickers. Additionally, we discuss how the photon rings are incomplete for the rotating boson stars considered, and how an unstable prograde light ring may be needed to remedy this.

</details>


### [3] [Black holes in a bouncing universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30818)
*Iara Pintos,Daniela Pérez,Florencia L. Vieyro*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究分析了黑洞群在反弹宇宙学中的收缩、反弹和膨胀阶段的演化，并开发了一个双流体相互作用模型，发现宇宙学流体会在固定几何的时空中改变其性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反弹宇宙学作为ΛCDM模型的替代方案，避免了初始奇点问题，但大尺度结构在收缩期会被抹除，而黑洞可能存续。研究动机是分析黑洞群在整个过程中的演化及其对背景宇宙学流体的影响。

Method: 开发了一个包含两种相互作用的流体的宇宙学模型，用于分析黑洞群在收缩、反弹和膨胀阶段的演化，并研究黑洞存在对背景宇宙学流体性质的影响。

Result: 研究发现，在固定几何的时空中，由于黑洞的存在，宇宙学流体会改变其性质。

Conclusion: 黑洞群可能在反弹宇宙学中存续并影响背景流体性质，这为反弹宇宙学模型提供了新的观测约束和理论见解。

Abstract: Bouncing cosmologies offer an alternative to the standard $Λ$CDM model by avoiding the problem of the initial cosmological singularity by construction. In these models, the universe undergoes a contraction phase that begins in a nearly flat and dilute state, followed by a bounce, after which the universe transitions into the expanding phase described by the $Λ$CDM model. During contraction, most large-scale structures are expected to be erased. Black holes, however, as shown by several previous investigations, may persist through the bounce.
  The goal of this work is to analyze the evolution of a black hole population throughout the contraction, bounce, and expansion phases. Additionally, we investigate how the presence of black holes influences the properties of the background cosmological fluid. To this end, we develop a cosmological model involving two interacting fluids. Our findings indicate that the cosmological fluid alters its properties in a spacetime with fixed geometry.

</details>


### [4] [Scalarization and descalarization in hyperbolic encounters of black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30865)
*Frederick C. L. Pardoe,Helvi Witek*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过数值相对论研究二次标量高斯-玻内特引力中黑洞双曲相遇激发的标量场演化，发现初始无法维持标量毛发的黑洞在相遇期间会经历动态标量化，并且自旋变化可导致永久性自旋诱导标量化或去标量化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究二次标量高斯-玻内特引力中黑洞双曲相遇过程中标量场的动力学行为，特别是动态标量化和自旋诱导标量化的可能性。

Method: 采用解耦极限方法，在背景度规上对标量场进行演化，运用数值相对论模拟黑洞双曲相遇过程。

Result: 初始无法维持标量毛发的黑洞在相遇期间可暂时标量化（动态标量化）；自旋变化可导致永久性自旋诱导标量化或去标量化（自旋上标量化/去标量化）。

Conclusion: 在二次标量高斯-玻内特引力中，黑洞双曲相遇能激发动态标量化和自旋诱导（去）标量化现象，且正负耦合均有可能实现。

Abstract: We use numerical relativity to study the scalar field evolution sourced by hyperbolic encounters of black holes in quadratic scalar Gauss-Bonnet gravity. In this theory, single black holes are known to acquire a scalar hair through scalarization for certain values of their mass and spin. We work in the decoupling limit and evolve the scalar field on top of a background metric. Seeding binary black holes with an initial scalar field, we find that configurations which initially cannot sustain a scalar hair temporarily scalarize during an encounter and thereby exhibit dynamical scalarization. This is possible for both positive and negative couplings between the scalar field and curvature in black hole binaries with zero and non-zero initial spins, respectively. Furthermore, we find that the change in the spin magnitude of black holes during certain hyperbolic encounters can lead to permanent spin-induced scalarization (or descalarization), which we refer to as spin-up (de)scalarization.

</details>


### [5] [A rotating black hole in a Hernquist dark matter halo: horizon geometry, thermodynamics, and quantum emission](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30962)
*A. A. Araújo Filho,Arun Kumar,N. Heidari,C. F. S. Pereira,Amilcar R. Queiroz,V. B. Bezerra*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 研究了一个沉浸在Hernquist暗物质晕中的旋转黑洞的几何、热力学和量子发射性质。通过非复化形式的新曼-贾尼斯算法构建旋转解，分析了晕参数ρ和旋转参数a对事件视界、能层、表面引力、霍金温度、熵、热容、量子隧穿率、霍金辐射和蒸发时间的影响。发现暗物质晕会推远事件视界、抑制温度、增加熵、改变热稳定性并延缓蒸发。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑洞研究多考虑真空或简单物质环境，而实际黑洞可能沉浸在暗物质晕中。本文旨在探究Hernquist暗物质晕分布对旋转黑洞的几何、热力学和量子发射性质的定量影响，以更接近真实宇宙中的黑洞物理。

Method: 从静态Schwarzschild黑洞嵌入Hernquist暗物质晕的度规出发，采用非复化形式的新曼-贾尼斯算法构造旋转解；通过求解径向函数Δ(r)的根确定视界结构，通过g_{tt}=0确定静态极限面和能层区域；利用表面引力导出霍金温度、贝肯斯坦-霍金熵和热容；通过哈密顿-雅可比方法计算量子隧穿率和粒子产生密度；利用斯特藩-玻尔兹曼近似估计霍金辐射、蒸发时间和光谱发射率。

Result: Hernquist暗物质晕将外事件视界推向更大半径，改变能层大小；旋转参数控制视界扁率及参考系拖曳强度；暗物质晕增大零角动量观测者的角速度；晕抑制霍金温度、增加熵，并通过Davies型临界点改变局部热稳定性；在弱晕慢旋近似下，暗物质晕降低霍金辐射光度并延缓蒸发过程。所有结果在极限条件下恢复标准Kerr和Schwarzschild解。

Conclusion: 暗物质晕显著影响旋转黑洞的几何、热力学和量子发射特性，延缓黑洞蒸发，在弱晕慢旋下辐射减弱；该研究建立了从真空黑洞到暗物质环境黑洞的桥梁，对暗物质间接探测和黑洞天体物理具有参考意义。

Abstract: We investigate the geometrical, thermodynamic, and quantum emission properties of a rotating black hole immersed in a Hernquist dark matter halo. Starting from a static black hole spacetime surrounded by a Hernquist distribution, we construct its rotating counterpart through the noncomplexification formulation of the Newman-Janis algorithm and analyze the modifications induced by the halo parameter $ρ$ and the rotation parameter $a$. The horizon structure is determined from the roots of the radial function $Δ(r)$, while the stationary limit surfaces and the corresponding ergoregions are obtained from the condition $g_{tt}=0$. We show that the Hernquist contribution displaces the outer event horizon toward larger radii and modifies the size of the ergoregion, whereas rotation controls the oblateness of the horizon and the strength of frame dragging. The angular velocity of zero angular momentum observers is also increased by the surrounding matter distribution. We further derive the surface gravity, Hawking temperature, Bekenstein-Hawking entropy, and heat capacity, showing that the dark matter halo suppresses the temperature, increases the entropy, and changes the local thermal stability through a Davies-type critical point. The quantum tunneling rate is obtained from the Hamilton-Jacobi method, leading to the corresponding occupation number and particle creation density. Finally, we estimate the Hawking luminosity (radiation), evaporation time, and spectral emission rates within a Stefan-Boltzmann approximation. In the weak halo and slow rotation regime, the Hernquist distribution reduces the luminosity and delays the evaporation process. All standard Kerr and Schwarzschild results are recovered in the appropriate limiting cases.

</details>


### [6] [Repetitive Penrose process for charged particles in Kerr-Newman black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30969)
*Mohammad Reza Alipour,Saeed Noori Gashti,Mohammad Ali S. Afshar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了极端Kerr-Newman黑洞中带电粒子的重复Penrose过程，建立了非线性迭代框架，通过三重转折点条件解析求解守恒方程，揭示了两个电磁耦合参数对过程演化的控制作用，并发现该黑洞可穿越中性态并反转电荷符号而不违反面积定理或宇宙监督假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究极端Kerr-Newman黑洞中重复Penrose过程的完整动力学演化，特别是带电粒子提取黑洞能量过程中黑洞参数的自洽更新机制，以及检验Reissner-Nordström情形中发现的放电屏障是否具有普适性。

Method: 建立非线性迭代框架，每次提取事件后更新黑洞质量、角动量、电荷和不可约质量；通过三重转折点条件获得守恒方程的解析解；分析两个电磁耦合参数$\hat Q\hat q_0$和$\hat Q\hat q_1$对动力学过程的控制作用。

Result: 确定了捕获粒子电荷参数空间中的四区域结构；发现了吸引相互作用($\hat Q\hat q_1<0$)显著增强能量回报率和能量利用效率；在临界电荷$\hat q_1\simeq-54.85405$附近逼近可逆的Christodoulou-Ruffini极限；发现了Kerr-Newman黑洞可穿越中性态并反转电荷符号，不同于Reissner-Nordström情形。

Conclusion: Reissner-Nordström黑洞中的放电屏障并非带电黑洞的普适性质；Kerr-Newman黑洞的重复Penrose过程可在不违反面积定理或宇宙监督假设的前提下实现电荷符号反转；建立了更完整的带电黑洞能量提取理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate the repetitive Penrose process for charged particles in an initially extremal Kerr--Newman black hole and develop a nonlinear iterative framework in which the black-hole mass, angular momentum, electric charge, and irreducible mass are updated after every extraction event. By imposing the triple turning-point condition, we obtain an analytic solution of the conservation equations, allowing the entire extraction sequence to be followed self-consistently. The dynamics are governed by two electromagnetic couplings. The coupling $\hat Q\hat q_0$ determines whether the incident particle can continue to access the ergoregion and therefore controls the termination of the repetitive process, whereas $\hat Q\hat q_1$ governs the depth of the negative-energy states and the extraction efficiency. An attractive interaction ($\hat Q\hat q_1<0$) significantly enhances both the energy return on investment and the energy utilization efficiency and, above a critical charge, produces a transient increase of the dimensionless spin despite the continuous loss of angular momentum. We identify a four-region structure in the captured-particle charge parameter space. Near the critical charge $\hat q_1\simeq-54.85405$, the evolution approaches the reversible Christodoulou--Ruffini limit with the energy utilization efficiency approaching unity while the black hole remains sub-extremal. Beyond this point the irreducible mass decreases, indicating the breakdown of the test-particle approximation. Unlike the repetitive Penrose process in the extremal Reissner--Nordström spacetime, the Kerr--Newman black hole can evolve through the neutral state and reverse the sign of its electric charge without violating the area theorem or cosmic censorship, demonstrating that the discharge barrier found in the Reissner--Nordström case is not a generic property of charged black holes.

</details>


### [7] [Phase space quantization of anisotropic cosmologies: Taub and Kantowski-Sachs models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31049)
*Jasel Berra-Montiel,Alberto Molgado,Jorge Santacruz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在相空间形变量子化框架下，对均匀但各向异性的Taub和Kantowski-Sachs宇宙学模型构造了非对角和对角Wigner分布的显式表达。通过Weyl量子化映射和Moyal星积解决了Wheeler-DeWitt方程中的因子排序歧义和星积形式收敛问题，并从对角Wigner分布恢复了标准波函数（修正Bessel函数形式），建立了与常规量子宇宙学的严格联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Wheeler-DeWitt方程在量子化这些各向异性宇宙模型时存在因子排序歧义问题，且星积形式通常存在收敛困难，需要一种无歧义的量子化方案来克服这些根本性障碍。

Method: 采用完全对称的Weyl量子化映射和Moyal星积，通过哈密顿约束的正则分离解决星积收敛问题，进而构造非对角和对角Wigner分布。

Result: 成功构造了Taub和Kantowski-Sachs模型的非对角和对角Wigner分布；从对角Wigner分布恢复的标准波函数与修正Bessel函数形式一致，与常规量子宇宙学结果相符。

Conclusion: 相空间形变量子化为各向异性宇宙模型提供了一种无因子排序歧义的量子化方案，且通过Wigner分布与标准波函数的对应关系，建立了与常规量子宇宙学的严格连接。

Abstract: We introduce an explicit construction of the non-diagonal and diagonal Wigner distributions for the homogeneous but anisotropic Taub and Kantowski-Sachs cosmological models within the framework of phase space deformation quantization. Conventional canonical quantization of these models via the Wheeler-DeWitt equation is inherently plagued by factor ordering ambiguities. To circumvent these issues, we employ the totally symmetric Weyl quantization map and the Moyal star product. By means of a canonical separation of the Hamiltonian constraint, we are able to resolve the formal convergence problems typically associated with the star product. Furthermore, to establish a rigorous connection with conventional quantum cosmology, we calculate the standard wave functions directly from the diagonal Wigner distributions, recovering the exact physical states in terms of modified Bessel functions in both cases.

</details>


### [8] [Geometric formulation for Palatini-Cartan gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31070)
*Jasel Berra-Montiel,Iván Cortes-Cruz,Alberto Molgado*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文从多几何-协变形式论的角度系统分析了四维Palatini-Cartan引力模型，包括拉格朗日层面的场方程与规范对称性、多辛框架下的动量映射与Cauchy数据、多规范框架下的Dirac-Poisson括号，以及时空分解后的瞬时Dirac-Hamiltonian形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受理解广义相对论相关物理模型的协变结构的需求驱动，旨在利用不同几何框架系统分析Palatini-Cartan引力模型的协变形式论。

Method: 采用拉格朗日形式论、多辛方法、多规范框架以及瞬时Dirac-Hamiltonian形式论等多种几何-协变形式论，对Palatini-Cartan引力模型进行综合分析。

Result: 在拉格朗日层面恢复了正确的场方程（无挠条件和爱因斯坦方程）；构造了规范对称群的拉格朗日动量映射及Noether流；在多辛框架下引入了诱导动量映射以恢复允许的Cauchy数据；在多规范框架中利用Moore-Penrose逆构造了非平凡Dirac-Poisson括号；通过时空分解恢复了瞬时拉格朗日量和扩展哈密顿量及规范结构。

Conclusion: 该工作系统地展示了Palatini-Cartan引力模型在不同几何-协变形式论下的完整结构，为理解引力理论的协变形式化提供了统一的数学框架。

Abstract: Motivated by the increasing efforts to understand the covariant structure of physical models associated with General Relativity using different kinds of geometric frameworks, in this article we analyze the four-dimensional Palatini-Cartan model for gravity, which is a well-known generalization of General Relativity, from the perspective of various geometric-covariant formalisms for classical field theory. At the Lagrangian level, we do not only recover the correct field equations of the theory, which are equivalent to the torsion-free condition and the Einstein equations, but we also study the gauge symmetries of the model in order to construct the Lagrangian momentum map associated with the action of the gauge symmetry group on the configuration space of the system and, consequently, its corresponding Noether currents. Within the multisymplectic approach, we analyze the action of the gauge symmetry group on the multi-momenta phase space of the model, and we also introduce the induced momentum map that allows us to recover the admissible Cauchy data of the system. Further, we also apply the algorithm to treat singular systems within the polysymplectic framework, in which, in order to obtain the correct field equations of the model, we introduce a non-trivial Dirac-Poisson bracket characterized by the generalized Moore-Penrose inverse of the matrix induced by the second class constraints of the system. Finally, using the multisymplectic framework as a starting point, we perform the space plus time decomposition of the system to recover the instantaneous Lagrangian and the extended Hamiltonian of the theory, as well as the gauge structure that characterize the Palatini-Cartan model for gravity within the instantaneous Dirac-Hamiltonian formalism.

</details>


### [9] [Stability of the Minkowski spacetime in Newman-Unti gauge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31090)
*Jonathan Luk,Sung-Jin Oh,Claude Warnick*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明了在中心归一化出射零测地线规范下，闵可夫斯基度规在爱因斯坦方程中的小数据全局稳定性。通过Dafermos-Rodnianski的r^p估计控制Weyl张量的解耦张量波动方程分量，其余几何量由输运方程控制，该方法适用于弱衰减到平直空间的初始数据，并可在数据具有更多结构时建立额外渐近控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 证明爱因斯坦方程中闵可夫斯基解的小数据全局稳定性，特别是在中心归一化出射零测地线规范下，并处理仅弱衰减到平直空间的初始数据。

Method: 使用Dafermos-Rodnianski的r^p估计来控制Weyl张量中满足解耦张量波动方程的分量，然后通过输运方程控制其余几何量，初始条件取自正则中心轴。

Result: 建立了对于仅弱衰减到平直空间的初始数据的全局稳定性，并在数据具有更多结构时可获得额外的渐近控制。

Conclusion: 该方案通过将Weyl张量分量与其余几何量分别处理，有效证明了弱衰减初始数据下的全局稳定性，并具有处理更结构化数据的扩展能力。

Abstract: We prove small-data global stability of the Minkowski solution to Einstein's equations in a centre-normalised outgoing null-geodesic gauge. Our scheme involves first using the $r^p$-estimates of Dafermos-Rodnianski to control certain components of the Weyl tensor which satisfy a decoupled tensorial wave equation. Having established this control, all remaining geometric quantities are controlled by transport equations, taking initial conditions at a regular central axis. This method establishes global stability for initial data which decay only weakly to flat space and can establish additional asymptotic control when the data are assumed to have more structure.

</details>


### [10] [On the Kalb-Ramond modified Lorentz violating hairy black holes and Thorne's hoop conjecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31116)
*K. K. Nandi,R. N. Izmailov,R. Kh. Karimov,A. A. Potapov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文放宽了能量条件，数值探索了Kalb-Ramond模型中洛伦兹破缺（LV）Schwarzschild黑洞的视界模式，发现了四类广义黑洞，包括与Randall-Sundrum膜世界黑洞（ρ<0）的类比，其中参数Υ被重新解释为“潮汐荷”。研究表明，除Schwarzschild-de Sitter型及其推广外，其余三类黑洞均满足Thorne's hoop猜想；膜世界潮汐荷黑洞会增大LV修正对行星近日点进动的影响，而普通黑洞则减小该效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究仅在满足能量条件（ρ>0）的特定LV参数范围内分析了Kalb-Ramond模型中的静态球对称Schwarzschild黑洞，但存在大量不满足能量条件的已知黑洞，因此需要放宽能量条件，探索更广义的LV修正黑洞家族的视界结构。

Method: 数值方法探索广义LV修正黑洞的视界模式，分析Thorne's hoop猜想成立条件，并计算行星近日点进动的LV修正。

Result: 识别出四类LV修正黑洞，其中一类与膜世界黑洞类比，Υ可解释为“潮汐荷”；三类黑洞满足hoop猜想，但Schwarzschild-de Sitter型及其推广不满足；膜世界潮汐荷黑洞增大近日点进动LV修正，普通黑洞则减小。

Conclusion: 能量条件的放宽揭示了更丰富的LV黑洞分类，hoop猜想的成立与否与黑洞类型相关；膜世界与普通黑洞对近日点进动的LV修正呈现相反效应，提供了两者的定性区分。

Abstract: Recently, a class of static spherically symmetric power law corrected Lorentz violating (LV) Schwarzschild black holes in the Kalb-Ramond model have been derived and studied in the specific range of LV parameters ($0<λ\leq 2,Υ\geq 0$) that correspond to energy condition preserving ($ρ>0$) source. On the other hand, there exist well known black holes that do not preserve the energy conditions. In this paper, we shall therefore relax energy conditions and numerically explore the horizon patterns of the enlarged class of LSMA black holes. Four generic types of LV corrected black holes emerge, which interestingly include the analogue of the \textit{braneworld} black hole ($ρ<0$) lending to $Υ$ a new interpretation of "tidal charge" known as an imprint from the $5d$ bulk in the Randall-Sundrum scenario. We shall then show that Thorne's hoop conjecture, $\mathcal{H} \leq 1$, where $\mathcal{H}$ is the Hod function, consistently holds for three types and their generalizations. However, intriguingly, it turns out that, for the remaining type (viz., Schwarzschild-de Sitter and its generalizations), the hoop conjecture does \textit{not} hold. It is also shown that braneworld tidal charge black holes increases the LV correction to planetary perihelion advance in contrast to the decrease due to ordinary black holes thereby providing a qualitative distinction between them.

### [11] [Galactic microlensing by backreacted massless wormholes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31118)
*G. F. Akhtaryanova,R. Kh. Karimov,R. N. Izmailov,K. K. Nandi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了Kim & Lee带电虫洞作为暗晕天体在银河系微引力透镜中的新型应用。分析了带电虫洞的光线偏折角（4阶PPN）、透镜可观测效应（像位置、放大率、质心和时延）、光学深度和事件率等概率特征。关键发现：与Schwarzschild黑洞相比，带电虫洞的Paczyński光变曲线更暗，且在源星进入和离开爱因斯坦环时呈现特征性"凹槽"（gutters），随着电荷Q趋近极端极限，凹槽逐渐合并，爱因斯坦半径消失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Kim & Lee带电虫洞作为暗晕天体在银河系微引力透镜中的新型应用，检验是否存在不同于黑洞的微引力透镜信号，从而为探测虫洞这类理论上预言的时空结构提供观测依据。

Method: 首先分析带电虫洞的ADM质量和几何特性（标量荷α和电荷Q的影响）；然后计算至4阶后牛顿近似的光线偏折角；接着分析电荷Q对透镜观测量的影响（像位置、放大率、质心和时延）；最后基于虫洞透镜与银河系束缚或非束缚的假设，估计光学深度和事件率等概率特征。

Result: 带电虫洞与背景Ellis-Bronnikov虫洞一样具有零ADM质量；电荷Q引入非平凡红移函数并改变喉半径；与Schwarzschild黑洞相比，带电虫洞的Paczyński光变曲线更暗，且在源星进入和退出爱因斯坦环时出现特征性凹槽；当Q趋近极端极限r_th/√2时，爱因斯坦半径消失，凹槽逐渐合并。

Conclusion: 推测重新分析银河系微引力透镜的过往数据可能揭示带电虫洞的存在，为未来通过引力透镜观测检验虫洞假说提供了可操作的预测。

Abstract: We study here a novel application of Kim \& Lee charged wormholes assuming them to be dark halo objects playing the role of lenses in the Galactic microlensing with source stars belonging to the Galactic Bulge and the Large Magellanic Cloud. First, we observe that both the backreacted scalar ($α$) and electrically ($Q$) charged wormholes have the same zero ADM mass as has the background Ellis-Bronnikov wormhole having a special equation of state parameter $γ=-1$. In particular, we argue that, for $α\neq 0$, the solution formally resembles, but can at best be sourcewise different from, that of the background wormhole. The charge ($Q\neq 0$) thus provides an extra degree of freedom that introduces a non-trivial redshift function $Φ$ to the background, alters its throat radius to $r_{th}$, yet keeps the wormhole massless. Second, we focus on this electrically charged case and calculate the light deflection angle up to 4$^{th}$ PPN order, analyze the effect of $Q$ on the lensing observables such as the image positions, magnification, centroid and time delay of images of the source stars. Third, we analyze the probabilistic features such as optical depth and event rate estimated on the basis of the hypothesis that the wormhole lens could be bound or unbound to our Galaxy. Finally, we report an intriguing qualitative prediction that, compared to the Schwarzschild black hole, the Paczyński light curves of the electrically charged wormhole are much dimmer that also show characteristic gutters at the times the source enters and exits the Einstein ring. \textit{The gutters gradually come together as $Q$ approaches the extreme limit $r_{th}/\sqrt{2}$, at which the Einstein radius $R_{E}$ vanishes so that the source crosses it instantly.} It is speculated that re-analyzing past data on Galactic microlensing may betray the presence of charged wormholes.

### [12] [Quantum work extraction of an accelerated battery as an indicator of trajectory-modified vacuum fluctuations in Minkowski spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31120)
*Xiang Hao,Cheng-Tai Wu,Wei-Wei Zhang,Gao-Feng Gan,Tian-Xi Ren,Jia-Yin Shen,Yin-Zhong Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种加速Unruh-DeWitt电池的物理模型，研究其在匀速直线运动和匀速圆周运动两种轨迹下，有无反射边界时的量子功提取（ergotropy）。线性运动的渐近行为可展示与KMS条件相关的Unruh热性，且不受边界影响。低温时直线运动ergotropy更高，高温时圆周运动更适合估计Unruh效应。靠近边界时ergotropy出现显著振荡和瞬时峰值，远离边界则快速达到稳态；圆周运动可延长振荡演化，且随距离增大ergotropy逐渐饱和。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索不同运动轨迹（直线vs圆周）和边界条件对加速Unruh-DeWitt电池量子功提取（ergotropy）的影响，以ergotropy作为真空涨落被运动轨迹修饰的见证者，并研究其与Unruh效应、量子相干性的关系。

Method: 构建加速Unruh-DeWitt电池沿匀速直线和匀速圆周两种轨迹运动的物理模型，分别考虑有无反射边界平面。以ergotropy（最大量子功提取量）作为观测指标，分析其渐近行为、振荡特征及稳态值，并与Unruh温度、KMS条件、量子相干性进行关联。

Result: 1) 线性运动的渐近ergotropy可展示Unruh热性（满足KMS条件），且不受边界存在与否影响。2) 低温时直线运动ergotropy更高，高温时圆周运动更优。3) 特定加速度下两种轨迹的量子功提取量相同。4) 靠近边界时ergotropy出现显著振荡和瞬时峰值；远离边界时振荡被抑制，ergotropy快速达到稳态。5) 圆周运动会延长振荡演化，随轨迹与边界距离增大，渐近ergotropy逐步上升至饱和值。

Conclusion: 运动轨迹和边界条件显著影响加速Unruh-DeWitt电池的量子功提取。ergotropy可作为Unruh效应的有效探针，且其行为与量子相干性受轨迹修饰的真空涨落密切相关。不同运动模式在不同温度区间各有优势，靠近边界时的振荡现象源于边界对量子相干性的保护。

Abstract: We put forward a physical model of an accelerated Unruh-DeWitt battery moving along two distinct types of trajectories, namely a uniformly accelerated linear motion and a uniform circular motion. Each trajectory is considered without or with a reflecting boundary. The maximal amount of quantum work extraction, defined as the ergotropy, serves as a witness to vacuum fluctuations modified by motion trajectories. The asymptotic behavior of ergotropy in a linear motion can demonstrate the Unruh thermality with respect to the Kubo-Martin-Schwinger condition, which is independent of the presence of a boundary. Comparing two kinds of trajectories, we find that for a very low Unruh temperature, linear motion yields a high amount of ergotropy, while for a high temperature, circular motion becomes optimal for estimating the Unruh effect. For a certain acceleration, quantum work extraction is the same for two different trajectories. The observed ergotropy for the thermality is closely related to quantum coherence affected by trajectory-modified vacuum fluctuations. In the presence of a reflecting boundary plane, we study different ways for the dynamics of the ergotropy. When the battery moves near the boundary, the prominent oscillation of the ergotropy will happen and exhibit some large instantaneous peaks. The interesting phenomenon results from the protection of quantum coherence for the accelerated battery in the vicinity of the boundary. Far away from the boundary, the oscillation behavior can be suppressed and the ergotropy rapidly arrives at a steady value. By contrast, the circular motion contributes to prolonging the oscillation evolution. The asymptotic amount of the ergotropy can rise progressively up to a saturation value with increasing the distance from the circular trajectory to the boundary plane.

### [13] [Cosmological Stealth fields and Non-Equilibrium thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31180)
*Gilberto Aguilar-Pérez,Cuauhtemoc Campuzano,Víctor H. Cárdenas,Miguel Cruz,Joel Saavedra*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究非最小耦合隐身标量场在平坦FLRW背景下的非平衡热力学特性，发现隐身条件导致标量场运动满足广义Riccati方程，耗散压力作为热力学驱动项。系统存在由熵产生选择的热力学稳定吸引子和不稳定排斥子，并在(y,ω_eff)相空间中识别出与ζ=1/4相关的近临界区域。重构隐身势后，体粘滞实现显示不可逆熵产生驱动宇宙趋向渐近de Sitter态，隐身场跟踪耗散背景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索宇宙学隐身标量场与非平衡热力学之间的内在联系，理解隐身场在耗散宇宙学背景下的动力学行为及其热力学根源。

Method: 采用非最小耦合标量场模型，利用能量-动量张量恒为零的隐身条件推导标量场运动方程，将其转化为关于变量y=φ̇/(Hφ)的广义Riccati方程。通过相空间分析和熵产生原理研究系统的稳定性和分支结构，并重构隐身势。

Result: 隐身条件导致广义Riccati方程，耗散压力为驱动项；系统存在两个热力学分支（稳定吸引子和不稳定排斥子）；在(y,ω_eff)相空间中发现ζ=1/4近临界区域；体粘滞实现中不可逆熵产生驱动宇宙趋向渐近de Sitter态。

Conclusion: 隐身标量场可被解释为非平衡宇宙学演化中动态非平凡的热力学跟踪器，其动力学行为与熵产生机制密切相关。

Abstract: We investigate the connection between cosmological stealth scalar fields and non-equilibrium thermodynamics in a spatially flat Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) background. We consider a non-minimally coupled scalar field whose energy-momentum tensor vanishes identically, allowing the field to evolve on a dissipative cosmological background without producing gravitational backreaction. We show that the stealth condition leads to a generalized Riccati equation for the scalar-field kinematics, where the dissipative pressure acts as a thermodynamic driving term. In terms of the variable $y=\dotφ/(Hφ)$, the system admits two thermodynamic branches: a stable attractor selected by entropy production and an unstable repeller. We also construct the corresponding phase-space structure in the $(y,ω_{\rm eff})$ plane and identify a near-critical regime associated with $ζ=1/4$. Finally, we reconstruct the stealth potential and present a bulk viscous realization in which irreversible entropy production drives the universe toward an asymptotic de Sitter state while the stealth field tracks the dissipative background. Our results suggest that stealth fields can be interpreted as dynamically non-trivial thermodynamic trackers of non-equilibrium cosmological evolution.

### [14] [Semiclassical Backreaction of Massive Quantum Fields in the Spacetime of a Global Monopole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31255)
*Owen Pavel Fernández Piedra*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 研究了点状整体单极子时空中大质量标量场、旋量场和矢量场的前导半经典反作用，发现量子源按$r^{-6}$衰减，诱导$r^{-4}$阶度规修正，其中标量场产生不同的时间与径向度规函数，而旋量场和矢量场导致单函数几何；量子反作用仅局部变形单极子外部，不改变渐近立体角亏损。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨整体单极子背景下的半经典反作用效应，理解量子场对时空几何的反作用如何修正单极子的经典结构。

Method: 利用Schwinger--DeWitt近似获得重整化的应力-能量张量，推导一般守恒对角源的半经典几何一阶解，并特化到自旋0、1/2和1的场。

Result: 量子源按$r^{-6}$衰减，度规修正达$r^{-4}$阶；标量场产生不同时间与径向度规函数，旋量和矢量场产生单函数几何；量子反作用局部变形单极子外部，不改变渐近立体角亏损。

Conclusion: 半经典反作用不会改变整体单极子的渐近拓扑结构（立体角亏损），仅在其外部区域产生局部几何变形。

Abstract: We study the leading semiclassical backreaction of massive scalar, spinor, and vector fields in the spacetime of a pointlike global monopole. Starting from the renormalized stress-energy tensors obtained in the Schwinger--DeWitt approximation, we derive the first-order semiclassical geometry generated by a general conserved diagonal source and then specialize it to fields of spin $0$, $1/2$, and $1$. The locally fixed quantum source falls as $r^{-6}$ and induces metric corrections of order $r^{-4}$. The scalar field generically produces distinct temporal and radial metric functions, whereas the spinor and vector fields lead to one-function geometries. We analyze the resulting curvature correction, the acceleration of static observers, geodesic motion, and the validity domain of the first-order solution. The quantum backreaction produces a local deformation of the monopole exterior but does not modify its asymptotic solid-angle deficit.

### [15] [Fragility of stealth solutions in mimetic gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31274)
*Alireza Allahyari,Clarisse Donio,Mohammad Ali Gorji,Zahra Gorji,Javad T. Firouzjaee*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类受约束的拟度规扩展引力理论，其中拉格朗日乘子场约束了度规与物质场的耦合。重点分析了$\bar{\lambda}\to 0$分支的屏蔽效应和$\bar{\lambda}=0$的隐形分支，发现后者在背景动力学上与广义相对论简并，但其扰动理论具有非均匀极限，导致屏蔽机制存在微扰病态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索一类包含拉格朗日乘子约束的广义相对论扩展理论，研究其屏蔽机制（在局域尺度恢复为GR）以及隐形解的存在性，并检验该屏蔽机制的微扰一致性。

Method: 通过作用量变分建立理论框架，引入标量场实现显式模型（$C=g^{\mu\nu}\partial_\mu\varphi\partial_\nu\varphi\pm1=0$对应Hamilton-Jacobi方程），利用Carter可分离性构造隐形的Kerr度规，并在一般层面分析背景与扰动的简并性。

Result: (1) $\bar{\lambda}=0$分支上，约束扇区不贡献背景动力学，GR几何成为隐形解；(2) 构造了球形对称解和隐形的Kerr解；(3) $\bar{\lambda}=0$分支在扰动层面与GR简并，但$\bar{\lambda}\to0$极限非均匀，导致屏蔽机制在微扰论下病态。

Conclusion: 所述约束扩展引力在隐形分支上虽能获得GR解，但其屏蔽极限在微扰论层面存在本质问题，限制了该机制作为有效屏蔽方案的应用。

Abstract: We study a broad class of constrained mimetic-type extensions of general relativity with action $S=\int{\rm d}^4x\sqrt{-g}\,\bigl(R/2+λ\,C[g,Ψ]+{\cal L}_{\rm m}\bigr)$, where $R$ is the Ricci scalar, $λ$ is a Lagrange multiplier, $C[g,Ψ]$ is a scalar functional of the metric and generic field content $Ψ$ (possibly involving $Ψ$ and its covariant derivatives) and ${\cal L}_{\rm m}$ is the matter Lagrangian. The branch $\barλ\to 0$, with the bar denoting a background value, provides a simple screening-like limit in which the constrained sector decouples, as in cosmological realizations where $\barλ$ is typically nonzero on large scales while locally one expects $\barλ\simeq 0$. On the exactly stealth branch $\barλ=0$, the constrained sector drops out of the background dynamics, so, on domains where a background profile $\barΨ$ satisfying $\bar C=0$ exists, the theory admits the corresponding general relativity geometries as stealth solutions. As an explicit realization of this mechanism, we consider the scalar field case, where $C=g^{μν}\partial_μφ\partial_νφ\pm1=0$ becomes a Hamilton-Jacobi equation selecting geodesic congruences; in this setting, we study spherically symmetric solutions and construct a stealth Kerr profile using Carter separability. We then show, at the general level, that the $\barλ=0$ branch is perturbatively degenerate with general relativity: the constrained sector contributes to the dynamics only through terms weighted by $\barλ$, which vanish on the stealth branch, while still imposing an infinite hierarchy of constraints on the fluctuations. Consequently, the $\barλ\to0$ limit is generically non-uniform, making the would-be screening perturbatively pathological.

</details>


### [16] [Distance duality relation in symmetric teleparallel gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31299)
*Rocco D'Agostino*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在对称遥平行理论中研究了距离对偶关系（DDR），证明在电磁场最小耦合且光子数守恒时标准Etherington关系仍然成立，但在非最小耦合f(Q)理论中光子数流不再守恒，导致DDR被动态破坏，并推导了广义DDR公式，发现DDR偏差与精细结构常数变化相关联，为区分几何与动力学起源的DDR破坏提供了统一框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在对称遥平行引力理论（非度规性媒介引力）中，距离对偶关系（DDR）是否成立，以及非最小耦合情形下DDR被破坏的机制，为未来高精度观测检验非黎曼几何引力提供理论基础。

Method: 从一般度规-仿射形式出发，采用几何光学近似，分析标准Etherington关系在非度规性存在时的有效性；进而推广到f(Q)理论中电磁场与非度规标量的非最小耦合情形，在同时规范下的均匀各向同性时空背景中推导广义DDR公式。

Result: (1) 电磁场最小耦合时光子数守恒，标准DDR成立；(2) 非最小耦合破坏光子数流守恒，导致DDR动态破坏；(3) 推导了广义DDR公式，建立了与Hubble膨胀率的直接联系；(4) 发现DDR偏差与有效精细结构常数变化之间存在关联；(5) 具体示例表明现象学可行的模型仅产生微小DDR偏离。

Conclusion: 该研究为区分几何起源与动力学起源的DDR破坏提供了统一理论框架，指出了利用未来高精度天文观测检验非黎曼引力理论的新途径。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the distance duality relation (DDR) in symmetric teleparallel theories, where gravity is mediated by nonmetricity. Starting from the general metric-affine formulation and adopting the geometrical optics approximation, we show that the standard Etherington reciprocity relation remains valid in the presence of nonmetricity when electromagnetism is minimally coupled and the photon number is conserved. We then extend the analysis to a class of $f(Q)$ theories with a nonminimal coupling between the electromagnetic field and the nonmetricity scalar. We demonstrate that such an interaction modifies the conservation of the photon number current, leading to a dynamical violation of the DDR. Focusing on a homogeneous and isotropic spacetime background in the coincident gauge, we derive a generalized DDR formula that directly relates observational distance measures to the Hubble expansion rate. Furthermore, we discuss the link between the deviations from Etherington's relation and variations of the effective fine-structure constant. Specific illustrative examples of the coupling function are also analyzed, showing that phenomenologically viable models predict only small deviations from the standard DDR. Our results provide a unified framework to distinguish between the geometric and dynamical origins of DDR violations, opening new avenues for testing non-Riemannian gravity with future high-precision astrophysical and cosmological observations.

</details>


### [17] [A parametric signal plus noise inference framework for short duration non-Gaussian noise transients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31304)
*Charlie Hoy,Ruxandra Bondarescu,Andrew Lundgren,Laura K. Nuttall*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文介绍bilby-antiglitch，一种在非高斯噪声中推断引力波源性质的方法，通过联合分析信号和噪声瞬变（glitch），能够在glitch污染数据中准确推断源性质，避免误判广义相对论违反，并验证引力波信号的真实性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统引力波分析假设噪声是平稳高斯的，但地面探测器中的非高斯噪声瞬变（glitches）常与天体物理信号重叠，导致推断结果偏差。需要一种能处理非高斯噪声的方法。

Method: 在贝叶斯推断框架中，引入准物理的glitch模型来描述短时非高斯噪声瞬变，将信号和噪声联合分析，开发bilby-antiglitch工具。

Result: 在被响亮glitch污染的模拟信号中，bilby-antiglitch能够准确推断真实的源性质，而传统技术会产生偏差；同时能防止对广义相对论的虚假违反声明。

Conclusion: 联合分析信号与glitch的方法有效解决了非高斯噪声对引力波参数估计的影响，验证了引力波信号在含有干扰数据中的异常真实性。

Abstract: Gravitational waves are now routinely detected with ground-based observatories, and, through a process known as Bayesian inference, their source properties are inferred. However, terrestrial noise artifacts, often referred to as glitches, commonly overlap astrophysical signals. This invalidates a fundamental assumption of gravitational wave analyses: the noise is no longer stationary and Gaussian. As a result, traditional techniques can provide biased inferences in realistic data. One method for mitigating the effect of glitches is to jointly analyse both the signal and noise in a single framework. In this work, we introduce bilby-antiglitch to infer the astrophysical signal properties in non-Gaussian noise. By additionally including a quasi-physical glitch model to describe short duration non-Gaussian noise transients, we show that unlike traditional techniques, we infer the true source properties of simulated signals contaminated with loud glitches. We also show that bilby-antiglitch prevents false violation claims of General Relativity, and validates the exceptional nature of gravitational wave signals in spurious data.

### [18] [Compactness Inference in Gravitational-Wave Mergers with PhenomDECO: Catalog Benchmarks and Robustness Diagnostics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31350)
*Shrobana Ghosh,Charlie Hoy,Mark Hannam,Frank Ohme*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过引入有效紧致参数C的phenomenological模型deco，对GWTC-3中所有高显著性双黑洞并合事件进行检验，发现大多数事件与BBH解释一致（C~0.5），但约20%事件出现低紧致度模式（C~0.15），这些模式源于低频噪声伪影，尤其在 Livingston 探测器中。唯一例外是GW231123，需在50Hz以上分析以消除低紧致度模式。研究强调低频数据处理对避免误判为奇异物理至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 部分引力波观测到的双黑洞并合事件中，成分质量挑战了传统形成模型，因此需要检验这些探测到的源是否确实符合黑洞双星（BBH）解释，而非其他奇异物理解释。

Method: 使用deco模型（基于有效紧致参数C的BBH模型现象学扩展），对GWTC-3中所有高显著性BBH事件进行后验分布分析，并利用时频残差（减去最大似然BBH和deco波形后）评估数据是否更符合基于紧致度的形变描述。

Result: 识别出三种后验形态：(i) 60%事件呈近高斯峰对应C~0.5；(ii) 部分事件有额外高紧致度支持(C≥0.8)；(iii) ~20%事件主导低紧致度模式(C~0.15)，该模式在提高起始频率后消失，表明对低频噪声敏感。除GW231123外，所有事件均与BBH一致。

Conclusion: 所有GWTC-3观测事件均与BBH源一致；低频数据处理在检验偏离BBH的异常信号时至关重要，为当前和未来引力波探测提供了基于紧致度的并合形态测试基准。

Abstract: Several gravitational wave (GW) observations have been identified as binary black hole (BBH) mergers, including systems with component masses that challenge typical formation scenarios. These observations motivate broader tests of whether the detected sources are consistent with this interpretation. We address this question using~\deco~, an existing phenomenological extension of a BBH model that uses an effective compactness parameter to characterize departures from the expected merger morphology. Applying this model to all high-significance BBH events from GWTC-3, we establish~\deco~as a robust test of the nature of compact binaries. In preliminary analyses we identify three recurring posterior morphologies: (i) near-Gaussian peaks consistent with the BBH expectation $C\sim0.5$, seen in 60\% of events; (ii) posteriors with additional high-compactness support $(C\ge0.8)$; and (iii) dominant low-compactness modes near $C\sim0.15$ in $\sim 20\%$ of cases. For the latter, the low-compactness modes disappear when the data, especially from Livingston, are analyzed from a higher starting frequency, indicating sensitivity to low-frequency noise artefacts. We further use time--frequency residuals, computed after subtracting maximum-likelihood BBH and~\deco~waveforms from the strain data, to assess if the data is better described by a compactness-based deformation. With this analysis, we conclude that all of the GWTC-3 observations that we have considered are indeed consistent with BBH sources. The exception is the high-mass GW231123 signal, for which data from \emph{both} detectors must be analyzed above 50Hz to remove a low-compactness mode. This study shows that low-frequency data treatment is crucial before attributing apparent deviations from BBH expectations to exotic physics, and provides a benchmark for compactness-based tests of merger morphology in current and future GW detections.

</details>


### [19] [Establishing Compactness as a Population Observable in Gravitational-Wave Astronomy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31364)
*Shrobana Ghosh,Charlie Hoy,Mark Hannam,Frank Ohme*

Conclusion: 紧致度可作为引力波天文学的关键可观测量，为区分黑洞与奇异致密天体提供新的诊断工具。

Abstract: Classically, black holes (BHs) are the most compact objects predicted in nature with C=0.5 in the Schwarzschild limit; C is defined as the mass-to-radius ratio in geometric units. In this work we perform a novel measurement on the nature of putative BH mergers in the gravitational wave (GW) data by directly probing the binary's closest approach through an effective compactness parameter. We confidently show all such high-significance signals in GWTC-3 are consistent with the BH hypothesis for the first time. Our hierarchical analysis yields $C_{\rm eff} = 0.5^{+0.3}_{-0.1}$, and we further limit the merger rate of low-compactness exotic binaries to $< 0.7\,{\rm Gpc}^{-3}\,{\rm yr}^{-1}$. This work establishes compactness as a key observable in GW astronomy.

This result suggests that dark energy may be a natural consequence of an early scale-invariant phase of the Universe.

The null-orbit structure admits an especially compact analytic treatment. The unstable photon orbit remains at the Schwarzschild-like coordinate radius throughout the black-hole branch, while the orbital frequency and Lyapunov exponent coincide exactly. Consequently, eikonal quasinormal modes (QNMs), shadow radius, GBFs, and strong-deflection observables are all governed by a single dimensionless function of the core-size parameter. The potentials of the point charge are found in quadratures throughout the space. To regularize the potentials, an approach motivated by the Shapiro effect for the time delay of radiation in a gravitational field is used. ### [24] [Rabinowitz Floer homology for Legendrian submanifolds in prequantization bundles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31674)
*Hanwool Bae,Jungsoo Kang,Sungho Kim*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立Rabinowitz Floer同调与量子同调之间的严格联系，为计算Lagrangian子流形的量子同调环提供新方法，并探索辛流形几何与拓扑填充障碍之间的关系。

Method: 利用预量子化丛Y上的Legendre提升L̂构造Rabinowitz Floer同调，通过Z_d-等变技术建立与L的量子同调的 isomorphism，并应用该同构进行具体计算与理论分析。

Result: 建立了Rabinowitz Floer同调与量子同调间的同构（环同构在更强条件下成立），成功计算了二次曲面和两步旗流形中Lagrangian球面的量子同调环，揭示了ω的量子可逆性与量子同调消失的关联，并证明了在存在极化且L与Lagrangian迹不交时量子同调为零。

Under the assumption that the minimal Maslov number $N_L$ of $L$ is greater than 2, we define the Rabinowitz Floer homology of $\mathcal{L}$. We then establish an isomorphism between the $\mathbb{Z}_d$-equivariant Rabinowitz Floer homology of $\mathcal{L}$ and the quantum homology of $L$, where $d$ is the degree of the covering map $\mathcal{L}\to L$. Under a more restrictive condition on $N_L$, we show that this map is a ring isomorphism. Using this isomorphism, we compute the quantum homology ring of Lagrangian spheres in quadrics and two-step flag manifolds. Furthermore, we investigate the implications of the quantum invertibility of $ω$ for the vanishing of the quantum homology of $L$ and the obstructions to topologically simple fillings of $\mathcal{L}$. We also show that if $(Σ,ω)$ admits a polarization and $L$ is disjoint from the Lagrangian trace, the quantum homology of $L$ vanishes.

### [25] [The auxiliary-deformed Breitenlhoner-Maison model: duality frames and higher-dimensional origin](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30717)

Motivation: 将经典可积的二维BM模型（即四维广义相对论在Kaluza-Klein约化后具有两个交换Killing等度规的可积子系统）通过辅助场方法（ν-框架）进行可积变形，并希望将这种变形提升到四维以探索其物理意义。

Method: 首先从ν-框架出发，推导互补的μ-框架辅助场视角；然后基于对偶不变拉格朗日形式（duality-invariant Lagrangian formulations of Einstein theory）的ansatz，将两种描述显式地提升到四维。

Result: 得到了一个四维变形模型，该模型是包含高阶导数的理论，但在ν-框架和μ-框架下都缺乏显式的微分同胚不变性。

Conclusion: 作者讨论了这种缺乏显式微分同胚不变性的可能解决方案，并探讨了该模型在四维中的物理诠释。

Abstract: The two-dimensional Breitenlohner-Maison (BM) model is a classically integrable subsector of $D=4$ general relativity endowed with two commuting Killing isometries, obtained via Kaluza-Klein reduction to $D=2$. Integrable deformations of such a theory have recently been constructed via auxiliary fields in the so-called $ν$-frame. In this work we first extend this point of view by deriving the complementary auxiliary field perspective known as $μ$-frame, and then explicitly construct the uplift to $D=4$ of both descriptions, relying on an ansatz inspired by duality-invariant Lagrangian formulations of Einstein theory. The resulting four-dimensional deformed model thus obtained is a higher-derivative theory which lacks manifest diffeomorphism invariance in both frames. We comment on possible resolutions of this puzzling feature and on the physical interpretation of the model in $D=4$.

### [27] [Complex Conformal Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30720)
*Yuma Furuta,Wataru Harada,Yuya Kusuki,Yin Tang*

Method: 将精确边缘耦合解析延拓到复平面，统一应用于体态、边界和缺陷形变；利用紧致自由玻色子作为可解模型揭示复高斯共形流形的全局结构；在Ising CFT中通过解析延拓研究一参数缺陷族，得到缺陷谱、能量传输系数和有效中心荷的精确表达式；通过AdS/BCFT对偶研究复边界重正化群流。

Abstract: Complex conformal field theories (CFTs) have recently emerged as essential frameworks for understanding non-Hermitian criticality, weakly first-order phase transitions, and walking renormalization group flows, while their general structures remain largely unknown. In this work, we propose a systematic construction of complex CFTs by analytically continuing exactly marginal couplings into the complex plane. This procedure applies uniformly to bulk, boundary, and defect deformations, preserving conformal symmetry while generically complexifying operator spectra and other universal data. Using the compact free boson as a solvable laboratory, we uncover the global structure of the complexified Gaussian conformal manifold. More generally, we demonstrate that genuinely complex rational CFTs do not exist: rational points remain confined to the real regime, providing a sharp distinction between real and complex theories. In the defect case, we investigate the one-parameter family of conformal defects in the Ising CFT and derive exact expressions for the defect spectrum, energy transmission coefficient, and effective central charge from analytic continuation. The theoretical predictions are precisely verified in non-Hermitian critical Ising and free fermion chains using bulk-defect correlators, entanglement entropy, and complex energy transport, providing concrete evidence for the complex defect conformal manifold. Finally, we study complex boundary renormalization-group flows through the AdS/BCFT correspondence. Our results establish complex conformal manifolds as a controlled bridge between solvable lattice models, complex CFTs, and holography, while providing stringent analytic benchmarks for the nonunitary conformal bootstrap.

Result: (1) 推导了任意度量挤压下自由能的普适二次响应正比于c_T系数，对幺正CFT证明球面自由能是局部最大值； (2) 守恒自旋s流的二次响应符号交替； (3) 给出Hopf纤维挤压的三次响应显式形式； (4) 得到标量算符两点函数的领头阶修正； (5) 在小纤维极限下建立了三维CFT与二维热有效作用量的对应关系，并确定了自由场、O(N)模型和全息CFT的Wilson系数。

Abstract: We study three-dimensional CFTs on compact Euclidean manifolds in two complementary limits: small deformations of the round $S^3$ and the small-fiber, large-squashing limit of Seifert manifolds. Near the round sphere, conformal perturbation theory expresses the free-energy response through integrated stress-tensor correlators. We derive a harmonic-space formula for the universal quadratic response to arbitrary metric squashing and show that it is proportional to the $c_T$ coefficient of the stress-tensor two-point function. For unitary CFTs this establishes that the sphere free energy is a local maximum in the space of metric deformations. This result extends to conserved spin-$s$ currents, whose quadratic response alternates in sign. For the specific case of squashing the Hopf fiber, we find an explicit form for the cubic response, and in addition obtain the leading correction to the two-point function of scalar operators. In the small-fiber limit, corresponding to the large temperature regime of the CFT, the partition function is governed by a two-dimensional thermal effective action constructed out of the Weyl-rescaled base metric and a Kaluza--Klein field strength. The thermal effective action relates CFT free energies on different backgrounds, including squashed Lens spaces, which we discuss in detail. We also explicitly determine the Wilson coefficients of this effective action, to various orders in the high-temperature expansion, for free fields, the large-$N$ critical O($N$) model, and holographic CFTs.

### [29] [Ryu-Takayanagi area from Virasoro modular data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30723)
*Jennifer Lin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文展示了在全息2d CFT中，多种全局态和子区域下的纠缠熵可以同时具有微观解释并与Ryu-Takayanagi公式的大c领头阶一致。通过将交叉对称性应用于复制流形，纠缠熵被重写为Virasoro代数在区域上的代数纠缠熵，其中中心标签通过对重原粒子的粗粒化获得。在大c极限下，鞍点近似主导求和，熵的O(c)部分来自主导bin中重原粒子的Cardy密度，被识别为Ryu-Takayanagi面积。这为RT面积的统计起源提供了具体物理解释，并给出了解释一致性所需的粗粒化程度的定量判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为全息对偶中的纠缠熵提供一个既有微观边界解释又与引力侧RT公式一致的统一框架，揭示RT面积的统计起源。

Method: 利用复制流形上的交叉对称性重写纠缠熵，将其表示为Virasoro代数代数纠缠熵的形式，通过将BCFT中重原粒子粗粒化到由Liouville动量标记的bin中实现微观解释，并在大c下通过鞍点近似求解。

Abstract: We show that in holographic 2d CFTs, the entanglement entropies across several choices of global state and subregion can be written in a way that at once has a microscopic interpretation and matches the leading large$-c$ organization of the Ryu-Takayanagi formula. This representation is obtained by applying crossing symmetry to the replica manifolds. From the boundary point of view, each rewritten entropy looks like an algebraic entanglement entropy for the Virasoro algebra restricted to the region, with center labels obtained by coarse-graining heavy primaries of the BCFT on the regulated region into bins labeled by Liouville momenta. At large $c$, a resulting sum over bins is dominated by a saddle, and the $O(c)$ part of the entropy comes from the Cardy density of heavy primaries in the dominant bin. We identify this $O(c)$ part of the entropy with the Ryu-Takayanagi area. Physically, this suggests a concrete statistical origin for the Ryu-Takayanagi area as coming from coarse-grained Virasoro intertwiners across the entangling cut. The result also provides quantitative criteria for the amount of coarse-graining allowed for the consistency of the interpretation.

Abstract: We develop a particle-on-a-group formulation of super-JT gravity aimed at computing supersymmetric correlators. We also quantize the reduced superparticle, with careful treatment of the fermionic constraints. We then derive the physical worldline supercharges from the requirement that the transformations preserve the constraints. These charges allow us to construct supersymmetric interval propagators in invariant variables and to formulate boundary-anchored Wilson-line operators for both superconformal primary and descendant insertions. Finally, we use these ingredients to build an algorithm for correlators. We obtain the $\mathcal N=2$ and $\mathcal N=4$ three-point composition kernels and zero-energy scalar three-point functions. For four-point functions, the same method reproduces the standard bosonic JT OTOC, gives an explicit zero-energy OTOC in $\mathcal N=2$ and $\mathcal N=4$ SJT, which is potentially useful for studying Berry curvature and BPS chaos.

Abstract: This paper explores the holographic Casimir effect associated with parallel spherical defects. The gravity dual is dominated by the AdS soliton with connected EOW branes at small widths, transitioning to AdS space with disconnected EOW branes as the width increases. Consequently, the holographic Casimir effect undergoes a first-order phase transition and vanishes in the disconnected phase. This new behavior highlights a significant difference from free theories, holographic parallel plane defects, and hyperbolic defects. Additionally, we confirm that the free theories adhere to the holographic bound for the Casimir effect in the case of parallel spherical defects.
  Interestingly, we observe that cosmic censorship provides a holographic interpretation of the attractive nature of the Casimir force when identical boundary conditions are imposed on both parallel surfaces. The repulsive Casimir force is associated with the bulk spacetime containing a naked singularity, which is generally considered forbidden. Additionally, we argue that topological censorship offers a natural explanation for why the vacuum of parallel defects is dual to the AdS soliton.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We study static, spherically symmetric screening solutions in the $\mathfrak{so}(N)$-invariant multi-field de Sitter Galileon theory, with matter couplings preserving the internal symmetry. Unlike in flat space, the de Sitter radial problem is affected both by the cosmological horizon and by the possible appearance of a finite strong-coupling radius, where the radial equation becomes singular and the effective description breaks down. Near the source, the quartic interaction governs the nonlinear screened branch, while farther away the quadratic terms dominate, defining a de Sitter analog of the Vainshtein radius at their crossover. A screened solution is viable only if this crossover occurs before the strong-coupling radius is reached. We study perturbations around the radial background and identify branches for which perturbations are stable and subluminal, within a restricted radial domain set by the strong-coupling point. Finally, we compare the de Sitter and Anti-de Sitter cases, isolating effects due to curvature from those specific to the cosmological horizon. Our results indicate that curvature can alleviate the superluminality issues that arise in Galileon theories for appropriate choices of matter couplings, though this comes at the price of a finite region of validity for the effective theory.

### [34] [Super $T\bar{T}$ deformation and the RNS non-critical superstring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30747)

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文回顾了超空间表述中N=(1,1)理论的超T\bar{T}形变，并结合非临界弦理论对其进行了诠释。通过将超空间方法与超黎曼曲面概念相结合，证明了超空间中的超T\bar{T}形变可以自然地解释为非临界RNS超弦理论。此外，文章还提出了一种可能的解释，即通过某些场重定义，将超T\bar{T}形变视为超空间中的二维超引力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在超对称背景下理解和诠释超T\bar{T}形变的几何与物理本质，特别是将其与非临界弦理论和二维超引力联系起来。

Method: 采用超空间表述方法，结合超黎曼曲面理论，通过场重定义建立超T\bar{T}形变与非临界RNS超弦理论及二维超引力之间的联系。

Result: 证明了超T\bar{T}形变可自然地解释为非临界RNS超弦理论，并提出了其作为二维超引力的可能诠释。

Conclusion: 超T\bar{T}形变在超空间框架下具有深刻的弦理论和引力诠释，为理解可积形变与量子引力的联系提供了新的视角。

Abstract: In this paper we review the super $T\bar{T}$ deformation of $\mathcal{N}=(1,1)$ theories in the superspace formulation, alongside its interpretation in the context of noncritical string theory. By combining the superspace approach with concepts from the study of super-Riemann surfaces, we demonstrate that super $T\bar{T}$ deformations in superspace can be naturally interpreted as a noncritical RNS superstring theory. We also propose a possible interpretation of the super $T\bar{T}$ deformations as 2D supergravity in the superspace through some field redefinitions.

### [35] [Fate of "Space-like singularities" in $c=1$ Matrix Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31925)
*Sumit R. Das,Shaun D. Hampton,Sinong Liu,Gautam Mandal*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究二维弦理论中超光速Liouville壁背景在双缩放极限下的奇异性问题。通过矩阵模型的量子淬火模拟，发现相空间密度在时间~O(log N)时受到IR壁影响，在~O(log N)²时费米面褶皱充分发展。利用作用-角变量证明相空间密度快速振荡，而粗粒化角度密度以普适幂律松弛到平衡态。表明类空奇异性是严格双缩放极限的假象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究二维弦理论中超光速Liouville壁背景在双缩放c=1矩阵模型中的动力学行为，特别是类空奇异性是否真实存在，以及非线性项在小N情况下的修正效应。

Method: 采用矩阵模型中的量子淬火方法，保留矩阵势的非线性项从而偏离双缩放极限；在费米子图像下使用Thomas-Fermi近似分析相空间密度演化；利用作用-角变量研究相空间密度的长时间行为。

Result: 早期相空间密度行为与双缩放理论一致；在O(log N)时间尺度IR壁效应显著；在O(log N)²时间尺度费米面褶皱广泛产生；粗粒化角度密度以普适幂律松弛到平衡态。

Conclusion: 类空奇异性是严格双缩放极限的假象；考虑非线性项后系统最终达到热平衡态；本文结果对弦理论中奇异性本质的理解提供了新视角。

Abstract: A class of time dependent backgrounds in two dimensional String Theory leads to superluminal Liouville walls on the worldsheet. In the dual double scaled $c=1$ matrix model these backgrounds involve eigenvalues leaking out to infinity, and the collective field fluctuations become strongly coupled along space-like regions, resembling singularities. We realize these backgrounds as results of quantum quenches in the matrix model, retaining non-linear terms in the matrix potential, thus departing from a double scaling limit. Working in the fermion picture in a Thomas-Fermi approximation, we show that while the early time behavior of the phase space density near the maximum of the potential agrees with that obtained in the double scaled theory, at times of the order $(\log N)$ the effect of the IR wall becomes significant. At later times, with a characteristic winding time of order $(\log N)^2$, folds on the fermi surface proliferate and eventually cover the allowed region in phase space densely. Using action-angle variables, we show that the phase space density oscillates around a time independent and angle independent value rapidly at late times. A coarse-grained density in the angle space relaxes to a time independent equilibrium value as a power law with a universal exponent largely independent of the details of the initial state. Thus, the appearance of a space-like singularity is an artifact of the strict double scaling limit. We comment on the interpretation of the final state in String Theory.

</details>


### [36] [On Black Holes Surrounded by Radiation: I. Classical Considerations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30794)
*Marcos Riojas,Matthew J. Strassler*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种名为"hillingar黑洞"的球对称静态解，它由Schwarzschild黑洞和周围由零径向压、无质量粒子组成的厚壳构成。这类解将光子球扩展为任意深度的区域，在经典层面上与普通黑洞在光学上难以区分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索一种新型黑洞解——被超紧凑、超相对论性无质量粒子壳包裹的Schwarzschild黑洞，研究其特殊性质及是否可能存在并区别于普通黑洞。

Method: 通过求解爱因斯坦场方程，构建球对称静态解，其中黑洞被零径向压的无质量粒子厚壳包裹，该气体可视为稳定爱因斯坦星团的边际稳定极限。

Result: 得到了"hillingar黑洞"解，该解将光子球扩展为任意深度区域；与其它气体包裹的黑洞相比具有诸多经典层面的特殊性质；从无穷远观测者视角来看，其光学特征与普通黑洞不可区分。

Conclusion: 这类物体可能在自然界中存在，尽管外观与普通黑洞相似但仍可能被观测到；其热力学和稳定性将在后续论文中探讨。

Abstract: We consider spherically symmetric static solutions to Einstein's equations describing a Schwarzschild black hole enveloped by a thick shell of orbiting massless particles with zero radial pressure. The orbiting gas is ultra-compact and ultra-relativistic, and can be viewed as the marginally stable limit of a stable Einstein cluster. These solutions, which we refer to as "hillingar black holes", extend the photon sphere into a region of arbitrary depth. We compare these objects to black holes surrounded by other gases and note they have numerous special properties at the classical level; in particular, they appear optically indistinguishable from ordinary black holes to observers at infinity.
  We speculate concerning the possibility that these objects (or others much like them) might exist in nature, and whether they might be observable despite their similar outward appearance to ordinary black holes. We examine their thermodynamics and stability in companion papers.

</details>


### [37] [On Black Holes Surrounded by Radiation II: Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30797)
*Marcos Riojas,Matthew J. Strassler*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了"希尔林加黑洞"（HBH）——一个被厚层无质量粒子海洋包裹的史瓦西黑洞——在热力学性质上对普通黑洞的模拟效应。研究发现，在热平衡假设下，HBH的温度和熵与相同ADM质量的普通黑洞相同。但在AdS空间中这种模拟不成立，且系统结构更丰富。此外，HBH可能在有限体积内蒸发，引发信息悖论问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究被无质量粒子海洋包裹的史瓦西黑洞（HBH）在热力学性质上是否与相同质量的普通黑洞一致，以及这种模拟效应在AdS空间中的表现，并探讨其与黑洞演化和信息悖论的潜在联系。

Method: 采用多种方法验证热平衡假设下HBH的热力学性质，包括温度、熵的计算与普通黑洞对比；在AdS空间中分析系统的结构变化；研究HBH在空腔中的蒸发行为。

Result: HBH在热平衡假设下具有与相同ADM质量普通黑洞相同的温度和熵；AdS空间中模拟不成立且结构更丰富；HBH在半径≥3M的空腔中可以蒸发，可能将信息悖论纳入有限体积中。

Conclusion: HBH在光学和热力学上均能模拟普通黑洞，但其作为实际黑洞模型的适用性尚不确定，不过可能与黑洞演化存在联系，特别是在有限体积内处理信息悖论方面。

Abstract: In a companion paper we considered a Schwarzschild black hole of mass $m$ enveloped by a thick "ocean'' of massless particles that extends the black hole's photon sphere into a region of finite depth. There we showed that this "hillingar black hole'', of ADM mass $M$, optically mimics an ordinary black hole of the same mass. Here we find it also mimics the black hole thermodynamically: the formal assumption of thermal equilibrium implies the system has the same temperature and entropy as an ordinary black hole of mass $M$. We check this result carefully using multiple methods; a further method and indications of metastability are given by one of us in a companion paper. In AdS space, the mimicry does not hold, and the solutions have a richer structure. While it is far from clear that these systems are models for more realistic ones, we note possible connections with black hole evolution. In particular, assuming thermal equilibrium can be established and maintained, an HBH in a cavity of radius $\geq 3M$ can evaporate, potentially posing the information puzzle in a small finite volume.

</details>

### [39] [As Cold as a Black Hole: Extended Photon Spheres](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30798)
*Marcos Riojas*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文挑战了“自引力辐射在渐近平坦时空中无法与黑洞达到热平衡”的普遍认知，发现了一个例外——通过分析光子球在Israel junction条件、TOV方程及有限半径黑洞热力学中的核心作用，描述了如何在不使用欧几里得路径积分的情况下计算粗粒化熵。关键发现是：在零径向压力下，IJCs和TOV方程精确等价；在固定质量下，在正比热区域添加壳层会降低渐近霍金温度。这个例外源于与M.J. Strassler的合作工作，其中发现的“hillingar黑洞”(HBH)可以模拟质量为M的普通史瓦西黑洞，共享其霍金温度、光子环及平衡态的粗粒化熵S=4πM²。研究表明这些特征并非调谐而成，而是由联合力学和热力学约束唯一确定。热力学模拟的充要条件由一个单参数自相似系统族满足，除HBH外，所有系统都需要在扩展光子球边界处存在无质量壁，这包括“最硬恒星”和“冻结恒星”。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战自引力辐射无法与黑洞达到热平衡的普遍认知，寻找例外情况并建立理论框架。

Method: 通过分析光子球在Israel junction条件、TOV方程及有限半径黑洞热力学中的作用，建立联合力学和热力学约束，推导热力学模拟的充要条件，并研究单参数自相似系统族。

Result: 发现IJCs和TOV方程在零径向压力下精确等价；在固定质量下，在正比热区域添加壳层降低渐近霍金温度；光子球处的逆比热与-Λ成正比。发现了hillingar黑洞(HBH)作为例外，能模拟普通史瓦西黑洞的热力学性质。

Conclusion: 自引力辐射与黑洞在渐近平坦时空中达到热平衡存在例外，HBH可以模拟史瓦西黑洞的热力学行为，其特征由联合力学和热力学约束唯一确定。热力学模拟的充要条件由一个单参数自相似系统族满足，包括HBH、“最硬恒星”和“冻结恒星”。

Abstract: It is widely believed that self-gravitating radiation cannot reach thermal equilibrium with a black hole in asymptotically flat spacetime. The following observation is used to describe an exception to this rule. The photon sphere controls central aspects of the Israel junction conditions (IJCs), the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff (TOV) equation, and finite-radius black hole thermodynamics. Through these results, we will describe how to compute coarse-grained entropies without using the Euclidean path integral. For instance, we find the IJCs and TOV equation are precisely equivalent at zero radial pressure. At fixed mass, adding shells in regions of positive specific heat lowers the asymptotic Hawking temperature, and the inverse specific heat at the photon sphere is proportional to $-Λ$.
  The exception described here results from companion work with M.J. Strassler, where we found that a "hillingar black hole" (HBH) mimics an ordinary Schwarzschild black hole of mass $M$, sharing its Hawking temperature, photon ring, and, in equilibrium, its coarse-grained entropy $S = 4 πM^2$. Here, we show these features are not tuned; they follow uniquely from joint mechanical and thermodynamic constraints. A necessary and sufficient condition for thermodynamic mimicry is found that is satisfied by a one parameter family of self-similar systems, all of which, excepting the HBH, require massless walls at the edges of their extended photon spheres. This family includes "stiffest stars" and "frozen stars".

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过动量空间热响应函数的适当正则化积分提取双扭结算符的热OPE系数；在4D全息CFT中采用AdS₅黑膜几何描述有限温度态，通过数值求解Klein-Gordon方程的径向ODE约化计算热响应函数。

Abstract: We explain how to extract thermal OPE coefficients of double-twist operators in scalar two-point functions at infinite spatial volume from suitably regularized integrals of thermal response functions in momentum space. As a specific application, we implement the proposed approach to four-dimensional holographic CFTs with an Einstein bulk action, where the finite-temperature state is captured by an AdS$_5$ black-brane geometry. In that case, the thermal response function can be computed on the gravitational side by solving numerically a radial ODE reduction of the Klein-Gordon equation. We obtain accurate values of double-twist data from this solution, completing previous holographic and bootstrap studies of thermal two-point functions. Some of the reported spin-resolved data that we compute are new.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 发现两类${\cal N}=(2,0)$超对称AdS$_3$解；构造了M5膜缠绕$\mathbb{WCP}^2_{[k,k,\ell]}$等加权投影空间以及纺锤纤维化于Riemann面上的解；全息中心荷与场论异常多项式和c-极值化结果一致。

Abstract: We classify AdS$_3$ solutions of the U(1) invariant sector of minimal $d=7$ supergravity. We find two classes of solutions preserving ${\cal N}=(2,0)$ supersymmetry for which the internal space M$_4$ is either a negative curvature Kahler-Einstein manifold or a circle fibration over $Σ\times \mathbb{R}$. For the later, in the case that $Σ$ has constant curvature, we reduce finding a solution to solving a single ODE that admits polynomial solutions. Among these are interesting solutions whose uplifts to $d=11$ describe M5 branes wrapping various $d=4$ orbifolds. These include a topological $\mathbb{CP}^2$ with 2 orbifold fixed points that we identify as the weighted projective space $\mathbb{WCP}^2_{[k,k,\ell]}$. We are also able to construct solutions with M5 branes that wrap a spindle fibred over constant curvature Riemann surfaces of arbitrary genus. Such solutions should provide holographic duals to the ${\cal N}=(2,0)$ SCFT associated to the M5 brane compactified to $d=2$ on these orbifolds.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于量子Bateman振子在非相对论性(2+1)维相位空间非对易框架下的形式化，利用自旋诱导的空间形变导出加倍量子动力学；构建SU(1,1)结构并解析放大的和阻尼的集体模；通过离散标度协方差分析自相似时间演化，并对振子扇区求迹得到约化动力学中的非马尔可夫记忆核。

Result: 无外部驱动下，系统展现出严格的自相似时间演化、对数螺旋轨迹几何表示、内在非马尔可夫记忆；机制依赖于非平衡约化动力学而非局域可观察量的平衡期望值，因此不受平衡时间晶体no-go定理约束。

Conclusion: 自旋是产生放大/阻尼Bateman动力学、自相似标度周期性、对数螺旋结构及非马尔可夫记忆的公共物理起源，该机制可自然推广至相对论性任意子体系。

Abstract: Can a closed quantum system generate time-crystal-like nonequilibrium behavior, self-similar scaling structures, and non-Markovian memory without external driving or coupling to a macroscopic environment? We address this question within the quantum Bateman oscillator formulated in a nonrelativistic (2 + 1)-dimensional phase-space noncommutative framework generated by spin-induced spatial deformation. The resulting doubled quantum dynamics is governed by a time-independent Hermitian Hamiltonian and exhibits an underlying SU(1, 1) structure with amplified and damped collective modes. We show that these modes satisfy an exact discrete scaling covariance, leading to self-similar temporal evolution without external driving. Upon tracing over one oscillator sector, the reduced dynamics becomes intrinsically non-Markovian and is governed by a history-dependent memory kernel. The same scaling structure admits a geometric representation in terms of logarithmic-spiral trajectories associated with the amplified and damped branches of the Bateman system. Because the mechanism relies on nonequilibrium reduced dynamics rather than equilibrium expectation values of local observables, it lies outside the assumptions underlying conventional no-go theorems for equilibrium time crystals. Our results identify spin as the common physical origin of the amplified and damped Bateman dynamics, self-similar scaling periodicity, logarithmic-spiral structures, and non-Markovian memory, also suggesting a natural extension of the mechanism to relativistic anyonic systems.

Abstract: We propose an asymptotic bootstrap method to evaluate moment integrals that arise in problems related to hermitian matrix models. These are normalized integrals of the form $a_n=\int^{\infty}_{-\infty} x^n \exp(-V(x)) dx$ where $V(x)$ is a polynomial of $x$. The method is applicable even when the coupling constants in $V(x)= x^{2\ell}/(2\ell) + g_{2\ell-2} x^{2\ell-2}/(2\ell-2) + \dots$ are complex. We prove that the method converges asymptotically exponentially fast on a cone region determined by the first subleading coupling $g_{2\ell-2}$, which must have a positive real part and an absolute value of the argument less than $π/{\ell}$. Abstract: In this paper, we investigate a fermion coupled to a Skyrme model in $2+1$ dimensions, where the Skyrmion is stabilized by the Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya and Skyrme interactions under a quadratic potential. Method: 通过解析构造可调能量密度分裂的双标量场翘曲背景；使用实轴相对概率谱和相移透射谱诊断共振；应用渐近迭代法（AIM）和时域演化（配合超对称伙伴势作为零模滤波工具）提取复频率平面中的类夸正则模。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate thick brane worlds in $f(R)$ gravity supported by two-scalar-field. The two-scalar sector provides an analytical warped background with tunable energy-density splitting, allowing us to test whether a Bloch-type internal structure can generate long-lived tensor perturbations resonances in the physically admissible region. We impose the positivity of \(f_R\equiv df/dR\), the derivative of the gravitational Lagrangian with respect to the Ricci scalar, which plays the role of an effective gravitational coupling in \(f(R)\) gravity. This separates the smooth ghost-free branch from a singular branch where this effective coupling vanishes. In the ghost-free branch, neither the relative-probability spectrum nor the phase-shift transmission spectrum shows narrow real-axis resonant peaks. These real-axis diagnostics indicate that the internal brane structure alone does not produce long-lived tensor resonances in the ghost-free region. Sharp quasi-localization peaks appear only in the singular branch, where the vanishing effective coupling induces divergent structures in the tensor potential; these peaks should therefore be interpreted as singular-boundary signals rather than ghost-free resonances of the smooth brane background. We then characterize the ghost-free massive Kaluza-Klein modes in the complex-frequency plane. Using the Asymptotic Iteration Method where applicable and time-domain evolutions with a supersymmetric partner potential as a zero-mode filtering tool, we extract the fundamental quasinormal frequencies. The modes have negative imaginary parts and quality factors \(Q\simeq0.9-1.9\), showing that the ghost-free massive tensor excitations are broad, short-lived dissipative modes. Thus the QNM spectrum provides the appropriate complex-frequency description of the Kaluza-Klein dynamics when no narrow real-axis resonances are resolved.

Treating these results as the unperturbed background, we analytically determine the higher curvature corrections to KK graviton spectrum and their couplings to Standard Model (SM) matter fields. We find that there is an appreciable upward shift in the KK graviton masses while leaving the graviton-SM couplings only mildly modified as compared to a model with only Einstein gravity in the bulk. However the net cross-section of processes involving virtual gravitons appears to be suppressed whereas the dilepton and diphoton decay widths of the gravitons are significantly enhanced because of the higher curvature corrections. Overall, these effects lead to observable modifications to both the production and decay signatures of massive KK gravitons and may be probed in some future precision collider experiments.

TL;DR: 本文研究了四维爱因斯坦引力中与中性标量场最小耦合的静态平面对称毛黑膜精确解析解，该解源于IIA型超引力的一致截断，描述了ABJM理论的强耦合热动力学。解由两个独立参数刻画，通过将标量毛发参数视为独立变量进行热力学描述，推导了广义第一定律并验证了欧拉关系。边界理论是受对数RG流形变的三维QFT，高温下显式破缺尺度对称性，但在红外热极限中恢复共形流体行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通过全息对偶研究强耦合规范理论的热动力学行为，特别是具有非平凡标量毛发的黑洞解及其边界场论的对偶描述。

Method: 求解四维爱因斯坦-标量引力场方程得到精确解析毛黑膜解，将其嵌入IIA型超引力的一致截断中；通过广义热力学第一定律和欧拉关系进行热力学分析；利用全息对偶研究边界QFT的重整化群流和尺度对称性破缺。

Result: 获得了具有两个独立参数的静态平面对称毛黑膜精确解；推导了包含标量毛发参数的广义热力学第一定律并验证了欧拉关系；边界理论表现为受对数RG流形变的三维QFT，高能区显式破缺尺度对称性，低能红外热极限恢复共形流体行为。

Conclusion: 该毛黑膜解为研究从尺度对称性破缺到共形恢复的热力学相变提供了全息框架，边界理论的红外极限表现为共形流体，与ABJM理论在强耦合下的预期行为一致。

Abstract: We study an exact analytic solution describing a static plane-symmetric hairy black brane in four-dimensional Einstein gravity minimally coupled to a neutral scalar, arising as a consistent truncation of the type IIA supergravity whose low-energy limit captures the strongly coupled thermal dynamics of the ABJM theory. The solution is characterized by two independent parameters. We perform the thermodynamic description by treating the scalar hair parameter as an independent variable, deriving the generalized first law and verifying the Euler relation. The UV boundary theory is a three-dimensional QFT at finite temperature deformed by a marginally relevant scalar operator with logarithmic RG flow. The boundary theory exhibits explicit scale-symmetry breaking at high energies but recovers the behavior of a conformal fluid in the infrared thermal limit.

</details>


### [53] [Convergence of Nekrasov instanton sum for unitary quivers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31953)
*Bruno Le Floch*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明了4维N=2规范理论Nekrasov配分函数的收敛半径在参数开稠密集上为正；对U(N) SQCD需b²∉[0,+∞)且库仑参数/质量避开超平面格点，对一般扭结仅需b²∉ℝ。渐近自由时收敛半径无穷大，共形时存在仅依赖b²的正下界。证明基于分割元组求和及组合不等式。通过AGT对应，这意味着球面或环面上Virasoro/W-代数共形块对一般维数和复中心荷具有正收敛半径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Nekrasov配分函数是规范理论中重要的生成函数，但其作为无穷级数的收敛性此前未被严格证明。明确其收敛半径对于理解瞬子展开的解析性质、AGT对应以及共形块分析至关重要。

Method: 将配分函数表示为分割元组上的求和，利用(余)钩长乘积的组合不等式证明级数的绝对收敛性。通过参数分情况讨论（SQCD/一般扭结，渐近自由/共形情形）给出收敛半径的精确估计。

Result: 建立了Nekrasov配分函数收敛半径的正性：渐近自由下无穷大，共形下存在仅依赖b²的正下界。对SQCD需b²∉[0,+∞)，对一般扭结需b²∉ℝ。AGT对应下这推出共形块的正收敛半径。

Conclusion: Nekrasov配分函数的瞬子展开在广泛参数区域内绝对收敛，为规范理论瞬子计算的解析性质提供了严格基础，并通过AGT对应推广到2d共形场论中。

Abstract: The convergence radius of Nekrasov partition functions (as a function of instanton counting parameters) is shown to be positive for 4d $\mathcal{N}=2$ quiver gauge theories with unitary gauge groups in an open dense subset of parameters. For $U(N)$ SQCD this is established if the ratio of equivariant parameters $b^2=ε_1/ε_2$ belongs to $\mathbb{C}\setminus[0,+\infty)$ and Coulomb parameters or masses are away from a lattice of hyperplanes. For general quivers it is only established for $b^2\in\mathbb{C}\setminus\mathbb{R}$. When gauge multiplets are asymptotically free, the radius is infinite, whereas in the (mass-deformed) conformal case the radius admits a positive lower bound that only depends on $b^2$. The proof relies on the expression of the partition function as a sum over tuples of partitions, and a proof of absolute convergence based on combinatorial inequalities on products of (co)hook lengths. Through the AGT correspondence this implies that large classes of Virasoro and W-algebra conformal blocks on the sphere or torus have positive convergence radius, for generic dimensions and complex central charges.

Result: 得到了从渐近平直区域过渡到近地平线几何的完整解析解，计算的修正熵与超对称指标方法的结果一致。

The solution interpolates between an asymptotically-flat region and the near-horizon geometry. ### [55] [The geometric bookkeeping guide for $\varepsilon$-factorised differential equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31994)
*Antonela Matijašić*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个系统的算法框架，用于为任意费曼积分族构建ε-因子化微分方程，该方法基于扭曲上同调理论和Baikov表示，通过两步实现：首先利用基于几何性质的排序算法（改进的Laporta算法）得到Laurent多项式形式的微分方程，然后通过系统构造变换矩阵实现ε-因子化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能物理中的精密预言需要精确计算多圈、多标度费曼积分，微分方程方法是标准工具，但只有在系统能化为ε-因子化形式时才能发挥全部威力。现有方法依赖于特定几何结构，缺乏适用于任意积分族的通用算法框架。

Method: 1) 在扭曲上同调框架和Baikov表示下研究费曼积分相关的微分形式空间；2) 引入基于几何性质的排序算法（改进的Laporta算法），对同一扇区内的费曼积分进行排序，得到具有Laurent多项式形式的微分方程；3) 系统构造变换矩阵，将系统化为ε-因子化形式。

Result: 该算法框架能够为任意费曼积分族（不依赖于底层几何结构）系统性地构建ε-因子化微分方程。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个通用的、不依赖于积分族几何性质的ε-因子化构造方案，有望进一步提升多圈费曼积分计算的自动化水平和效率。

Abstract: Precision predictions for high-energy experiments rely on accurately evaluating multi-loop, multi-scale Feynman integrals in dimensional regularisation. The method of differential equations is by now the standard tool for this task, but its full power is only realised when the system can be brought into an $\varepsilon$-factorised form. In this talk, we present an algorithmic framework that systematically constructs $\varepsilon$-factorised differential equations for arbitrary integral families, independent of their underlying geometry. We work in the setting of twisted cohomology and study the space of differential forms associated with a given family of Feynman integrals in the Baikov representation. Our approach consists of two steps. First, we introduce a particular ordering for the Laporta algorithm that orders Feynman integrals within a sector according to their geometric properties. We observe that this order relation yields a basis whose differential equation is in a Laurent polynomial form in the dimensional regulator $\varepsilon$. In the second step, we systematically construct transformation matrices such that the resulting system is in the $\varepsilon$-factorised form.
